SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Code], [t].[CreatedAt], [t].[ExpiryDate], [t].[IsActive], [t].[IsDeleted], [t].[LotNo], [t].[ProducedQuantity], [t].[ProductId], [t].[SerialStartValue], [t].[Status], [t].[TargetQuantity], [t].[UpdatedAt], [t].[Id0], [t].[Code0], [t].[CreatedAt0], [t].[CustomerId], [t].[GTIN], [t].[IsActive0], [t].[IsDeleted0], [t].[Name], [t].[UpdatedAt0], [s].[Id], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[IsActive], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[SN], [s].[SSCCId], [s].[UpdatedAt], [s].[WorkOrderId], [t0].[Id], [t0].[CreatedAt], [t0].[IsActive], [t0].[IsDeleted], [t0].[Level], [t0].[ParentSSCCId], [t0].[SSCCCode], [t0].[UpdatedAt], [t0].[WorkOrderId], [t0].[Id0], [t0].[CreatedAt0], [t0].[IsActive0], [t0].[IsDeleted0], [t0].[Level0], [t0].[ParentSSCCId0], [t0].[SSCCCode0], [t0].[UpdatedAt0], [t0].[WorkOrderId0]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [w].[Id], [w].[Code], [w].[CreatedAt], [w].[ExpiryDate], [w].[IsActive], [w].[IsDeleted], [w].[LotNo], [w].[ProducedQuantity], [w].[ProductId], [w].[SerialStartValue], [w].[Status], [w].[TargetQuantity], [w].[UpdatedAt], [p].[Id] AS [Id0], [p].[Code] AS [Code0], [p].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [p].[CustomerId], [p].[GTIN], [p].[IsActive] AS [IsActive0], [p].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted0], [p].[Name], [p].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0]
    FROM [WorkOrders] AS [w]
    INNER JOIN [Products] AS [p] ON [w].[ProductId] = [p].[Id]
    WHERE CONVERT(varchar(36), [w].[Id]) = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [SerialNumbers] AS [s] ON [t].[Id] = [s].[WorkOrderId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s0].[Id], [s0].[CreatedAt], [s0].[IsActive], [s0].[IsDeleted], [s0].[Level], [s0].[ParentSSCCId], [s0].[SSCCCode], [s0].[UpdatedAt], [s0].[WorkOrderId], [s1].[Id] AS [Id0], [s1].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [s1].[IsActive] AS [IsActive0], [s1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted0], [s1].[Level] AS [Level0], [s1].[ParentSSCCId] AS [ParentSSCCId0], [s1].[SSCCCode] AS [SSCCCode0], [s1].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0], [s1].[WorkOrderId] AS [WorkOrderId0]
    FROM [SSCCs] AS [s0]
    LEFT JOIN [SSCCs] AS [s1] ON [s0].[Id] = [s1].[ParentSSCCId]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[WorkOrderId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [s].[Id], [t0].[Id]
